CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS Beverage (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(255), brand VARCHAR(255), price DECIMAL(10, 2);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS Ingredient (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(255), category VARCHAR(255), price DECIMAL(10, 2);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS Menu (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(255), type VARCHAR(255), price DECIMAL(10, 2);</t><s>insert into food (id, name, category, price, quantity) select 1, 'pizza', 'fast food', 12.99, 10 from dual</s>

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS Beverage (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(255), brand VARCHAR(255), price DECIMAL(10, 2);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS Menu (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(255), type VARCHAR(255), price DECIMAL(10, 2);</t><s>insert into ingredient (id, name, category, price) select 1, 'flour', 'baking', 5.99 from dual</s>

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS Ingredient (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(255), category VARCHAR(255), price DECIMAL(10, 2);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS Food (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(255), category VARCHAR(255), price DECIMAL(10, 2), quantity INT);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS Beverage (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(255), brand VARCHAR(255), price DECIMAL(10, 2);</t><s>INSERT INTO Ingredient (id, name, category, price) SELECT 1, 'Flour', 'Baking', 5.99 FROM dual</s>

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS Ingredient (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(255), category VARCHAR(255), price DECIMAL(10, 2);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS Menu (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(255), type VARCHAR(255), price DECIMAL(10, 2);</t><s>insert into recipe (id, name, description) select 1, 'chocolate cake', 'delicious chocolate cake recipe' from dual</s>

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS Ingredient (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(255), category VARCHAR(255), price DECIMAL(10, 2);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS Food (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(255), category VARCHAR(255), price DECIMAL(10, 2), quantity INT);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS Beverage (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(255), brand VARCHAR(255), price DECIMAL(10, 2);</t><s>insert into recipe (id, name, description) select 1, 'chocolate cake', 'delicious chocolate cake recipe' from dual</s>

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS Recipe (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(255), description TEXT);</t><s>insert into menu (id, name, type, price) select 1, 'lunch special', 'main course', 19.99 from dual</s>
